APRIL'S FOOL

To the future I sent- The past we spent. The love I gave, The love I saved. In my heart's a room, For your lovely bloom. A room with your name, An irreplaceable space. No matter what time, even past nine, You can open those doors. For you can call me "mine", For I can call me "yours". If you leave or stay, I have one thing to say. Nothing will change, For I am your warm embrace. The love I saved, Is for your grace. The I love I gave, Is for your days. No matter the writing, No matter the lines, No matter the start, No matter the intent. Unsure of the ending, But sure of the end. I don't know the last page, But I know what's written. In the final days, In the final moments. My love I gave, The love I saved. It's for you, For all those days, in every second, minutes, I'm yours. Happy 9 months, my Love ^_^

TO RORI FROM HER LOYDIE
